name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Sheraton King Bed Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:6 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:The hotel rooms are quite distinctive. There is a small corridor at the entrance, with toilets and cloakrooms on both sides. At the end of the corridor is a screen, and behind the screen is the guest room. The layout of the guest room is quite simple (actually a bit too simple for this level). The room I stayed in on the shady side has a thin quilt and the room is not very warm. I have to turn on the air conditioner to sleep at night in winter.

The bathroom is average, the gym is average, the breakfast is average, the dining area is quite large but the dishes are not special. The view outside the window is pretty good. The villa area behind is pretty beautiful but it seems to be unfinished.

Among the five-star hotels in Changchun, Jingyue Sheraton is relatively remote, and there are no companies or schools nearby. According to my impression, the hotel does not have a high passenger flow (especially compared to its huge building volume), the hotel is relatively quiet inside and outside, and the price is relatively low.

msg:I really don't recommend staying here in winter. I read comments saying that the parent-child room was colder and the air conditioner was broken. I thought it was an isolated phenomenon. As a result, the room we stayed in was also broken. I didn't know it was broken on the first night, but I thought the temperature hadn't come up yet. As a result, the air conditioner didn't work all night. It was more than 20 degrees below zero outside, and the air conditioner in the room was not strong. The whole family was wearing thick clothes, covered with quilts and big down jackets, but they still felt cold... I really regretted booking for two days in a row. I wanted to cancel one night but couldn't, so I asked for an electric heater. It was finally warm on the second night, but the electric heater was really loud, but at least it wasn't cold... The room was big, but the hygiene was really not in place. It was dirty everywhere. The children's slides and plush toys should not have been cleaned. The children played with them and itched all over, but they didn't let them touch those toys. The waiter who checked in at the front desk that day was very unprofessional and indifferent. I don't know why. We were all polite, but she looked high and mighty. She didn't raise her eyelids to talk to you when she asked anything. It was in sharp contrast to the beautiful front desk lady at Hyatt on the first day... There was no at least courtesy! However, she was an isolated case. The other service staff I met during my two-day stay were very friendly.

At night, the child accidentally spilled mineral water on the bed. I asked the cleaning staff to come and change it. They came reluctantly and had a bad attitude.
